                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://2minutidodio.blogspot.it/2011/05/dal-profondo_19.html">
                      Dal Profondo (From The Deep)
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8001247373261084240" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ZaiM0UEbC6M/TdU1iwOBTdI/AAAAAAAAADk/0XPgQD97wHQ/s1600/Michel+Mandurino+-+Dall%2527Abisso+-+2011+-+tec.+collografia+monotipo+-+3+stampe+35x25+cm.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="380" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ZaiM0UEbC6M/TdU1iwOBTdI/AAAAAAAAADk/0XPgQD97wHQ/s640/Michel+Mandurino+-+Dall%2527Abisso+-+2011+-+tec.+collografia+monotipo+-+3+stampe+35x25+cm.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      "Dall'Abisso"(From The Abyss) 2011 Tec. collografia monotipo 3 stampe 35x25 cm
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--w3lzXxV_DM/TdU1lx10jgI/AAAAAAAAADo/UUtWt2faw6c/s1600/Michel+Mandurino+-+L%2527Altrove+-+2011+-+tec.collografia+monotipo+-+2+stampe+50x35+cm.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="412" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--w3lzXxV_DM/TdU1lx10jgI/AAAAAAAAADo/UUtWt2faw6c/s640/Michel+Mandurino+-+L%2527Altrove+-+2011+-+tec.collografia+monotipo+-+2+stampe+50x35+cm.jpg" width="640"/>

                     </div>

                    <meta content="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-tlDmtvcZ6vo/TdUwlJfI-4I/AAAAAAAAADc/KwJRZRWJ4ks/s400/Michel+Mandurino+R%2527lyeh+%25232+115x+145.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>

                    <meta content="4221564148625028515" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="4221564148625028515">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://2minutidodio.blogspot.it/2011/05/dal-profondo.html">
                      R'lyeh  l'irrapresentabile
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-4221564148625028515" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-tlDmtvcZ6vo/TdUwlJfI-4I/AAAAAAAAADc/KwJRZRWJ4ks/s1600/Michel+Mandurino+R%2527lyeh+%25232+115x+145.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="318" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-tlDmtvcZ6vo/TdUwlJfI-4I/AAAAAAAAADc/KwJRZRWJ4ks/s400/Michel+Mandurino+R%2527lyeh+%25232+115x+145.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      "R'lyeh #2" 2011 Tec. mista su carta intelata 115x145 cm
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3i7lUNJoX_A/TdUwjiBP_fI/AAAAAAAAADY/9cZfkqMmVkc/s1600/Michel+Mandurino+R%2527lyeh+%25231+95x120.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-3i7lUNJoX_A/TdUwjiBP_fI/AAAAAAAAADY/9cZfkqMmVkc/s400/Michel+Mandurino+R%2527lyeh+%25231+95x120.jpg" width="400"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      "R'lyeh #1" 2011 Tec. mista su carta intelata 95x120 cm
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <i>
                       Ci che mi affascina nel provare a rappresentareR'lyeh  che non si pu farlo.
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <i>
                       Certamente quello che ho voluto rappresentare in questi due lavori non  la ricerca descrittiva delle incredibili architetture ma la sensazione di spaesamento e l'offuscamento delle percezioni.
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <i>
                       <br/>
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <i>
                       Questo  solo l'inizio, rappresenter nuovamente l'incredibile citt in nuovi modi e con altre tecniche.
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <i>
                       RappresentareR'lyeh  una grande sfida.
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>

                      Dea Ancestrale, Grande Madre Inanna
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-13555955909096288" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-zv7_CZDx1Hg/TWPxc2V7GwI/AAAAAAAAADI/KOyD36elryI/s1600/Inanna+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">

                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   marted 28 dicembre 2010
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TRnXbzst55I/AAAAAAAAACo/yhl_jW4eDVM/s400/Chtulhu+F.+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="8171684714129784186" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="3589492799774786943" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="3589492799774786943">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://2minutidodio.blogspot.it/2010/12/phnglui-mglwnafh-cthulhu-rlyeh-wgahnagl.html">
                      Ph'nglui mglw'nafh Cthulhu R'lyeh wgah'nagl fhtagn!
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-3589492799774786943" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TRnXbzst55I/AAAAAAAAACo/yhl_jW4eDVM/s1600/Chtulhu+F.+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="400" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TRnXbzst55I/AAAAAAAAACo/yhl_jW4eDVM/s400/Chtulhu+F.+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" width="380"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      "Cthulhu" 2010 Tec. Cera policroma Dim. H 18 cm c.a.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TRnX64z3VII/AAAAAAAAACs/A3U8iL2aN_c/s1600/Chtulhu+P.+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <br/>
                      </a>
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TRnX64z3VII/AAAAAAAAACs/A3U8iL2aN_c/s1600/Chtulhu+P.+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TRnX64z3VII/AAAAAAAAACs/A3U8iL2aN_c/s1600/Chtulhu+P.+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TRnX64z3VII/AAAAAAAAACs/A3U8iL2aN_c/s320/Chtulhu+P.+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" width="300"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TRnYYnadU2I/AAAAAAAAACw/pzKzH5iokU0/s1600/Chtulhu+R.+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: right; float: right; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-left: 1em;">
                      <img border="0" height="320" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TRnYYnadU2I/AAAAAAAAACw/pzKzH5iokU0/s320/Chtulhu+R.+Michel+Mandurino.jpg" width="297"/>
                     </a>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, monospace;">
                      <i>
                       Una figura realizzata con palese intento pittorico, anche se l'esecuzione impressionista impediva di farsi una chiara idea della sua natura. sembrava una specie di mostro, e l'aspetto era quello che solo una fantasia malata potrebbe concepire. Non sar infedele allo spirito dell'icona se dico che la mia immaginazione, a volte un p bizzarra, se la raffigurava contemporaneamente come una piovra, un drago e una caricatura umana.
                      </i>
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, monospace;">
                      <i>
                       Una testa molle e tentacolata sormontava un corpo grottesco, scaglioso, con ali rudimentali; ma era
                       <b>
                        l'aspetto complessivoche
                       </b>
                       <b>
                        lo rendeva orribile
                       </b>
                       .
                      </i>
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, monospace;">
                      <i>
                       <br/>
                      </i>
                     </span>
                     <br/>
                     <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-family: 'Courier New', Courier, monospace;">
                      Tratto da "
                      <i>
                       Il richiamo di Cthulhu"
                      </i>
                      H.P Lovecraft
                     </span>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>

                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   domenica 28 novembre 2010
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TPK_378JsRI/AAAAAAAAACM/zBVHTKNYM7M/s400/dungeon-dungeon.JPG" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="8171684714129784186" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="779457623089147979" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="779457623089147979">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://2minutidodio.blogspot.it/2010/11/tristram.html">
                      Tristram
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-779457623089147979" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TPK_378JsRI/AAAAAAAAACM/zBVHTKNYM7M/s1600/dungeon-dungeon.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="400" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TPK_378JsRI/AAAAAAAAACM/zBVHTKNYM7M/s400/dungeon-dungeon.JPG" width="266"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      "Dungeon" 2010 Tec. Fotografia digitale
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <i>
                       In primavera di quest'anno mi sono recato al duomo di Firenze per scattare qualche foto all'altare maggiore, doveva servirmi come sfondo per un dipinto.
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <i>
                       Fatti gli scatti che mi servivano mi sono soffermato ad osservare i turisti che vagavano per la chiesa, sopratutto quelli che scendevano le scale per i sotterranei e scoprivano che l'accesso ai resti dell'antica chiesa di S. Reparata era chiuso (la grata serrata sulla sinistra) e l'unica cosa aperta era il negozio di souvenir sotterraneo.
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <i>
                       Era ipnotico osservare questo fiume di gente che scendeva incuriosito e risaliva arrabbiato.
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <i>
                       Dalla prospettiva da cui ho scattato la foto la luce del bazar di ciarpame da un atmosfera di discesa negli inferi ed ho usato un tempo lungo per far si che i poveri turisti raggirati si tramutassero in entit evanescenti.
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <i>
                       Guardando questo scatto mi  sembra di vedere l'entrata per il sottosuolo della cattedrale di Tristram.
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
                      <i>
                       <br/>
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <i>
                       <br/>
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div style="text-align: left;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="clear: both;">
                     </div>
                    </div>

                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://2minutidodio.blogspot.it/2010/11/la-seduzione-del-reale.html">
                      La Seduzione del Reale.
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-1225165555479270922" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TM6jrEU4IzI/AAAAAAAAABc/D8zv9tKXrLY/s1600/Ambra+(tec.+olio+su+carta+intelata)Michel+Mandurino+2010.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TM6jrEU4IzI/AAAAAAAAABc/D8zv9tKXrLY/s320/Ambra+(tec.+olio+su+carta+intelata)Michel+Mandurino+2010.JPG" width="242"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      "Ambra" 2010 Tec. Olio su carta intelata su lino 80x75 cm Priv. Col.
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TM6kPCcIoaI/AAAAAAAAABg/0Md1Nf96Lqk/s1600/Ombre+(tec.+olio+su+carta+intelata)+Michel.Mandurino+2010JPG.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="400" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TM6kPCcIoaI/AAAAAAAAABg/0Md1Nf96Lqk/s400/Ombre+(tec.+olio+su+carta+intelata)+Michel.Mandurino+2010JPG.JPG" width="247"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">

                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      "Ombre" 2010 Tec. Olio su carta intelata su lino 90x56 cm  Priv.Col. Mr. Thyper

                        <b>

                      <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: #2a2a2a; font-family: Tahoma, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <br style="line-height: 17px;"/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Schiudi per me le Porte deglInferi
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Ruba per me delleffimera Vita
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Le mere gioie ed i vani diletti
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Chio della Morte sorridere possa
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Il giorno in cui trover sopita
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       La mia giovinezza entro unumida fossa
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       <br style="line-height: 17px;"/>
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       E lieto avr sulle labbra
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Di vino e fumo bagnate
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       E dAfrodite le grazie
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Rime da savia follia disegnate
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Vita ho bevuta fino al sorso estremo
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Non ho rimpianti e Morte non temo
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       <br style="line-height: 17px;"/>
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Purpurea china
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Scarlatto inchiostro
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Sangue su tela nel quadro
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Che di te mostro
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Dolce Compagno
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Dallalma perduta
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       <br style="line-height: 17px;"/>
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Libero e fiero
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       E tra molti solingo
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Vaghi coi Figli del Buio
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       E come sparviero
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Privo di vincoli lali dispieghi
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Dun predatore ramingo
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       <br style="line-height: 17px;"/>
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Danime e affetti
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       E inermi rancori
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       E nude fanciulle di cui
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Con i colori diletti
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Entro un rifugio di tela racchiudi
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       I volti ed i giovani cuori
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       <br style="line-height: 17px;"/>
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       A te i miei versi
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Mio buon amico
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Mentre alla voce
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Ed al cuore concedo
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Ci che ad un dono di carta e rima fugace
                      </i>
                     </div>
                     <div align="CENTER" style="line-height: 17px; margin-bottom: 0cm; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;">
                      <i>
                       Oggi non dico
                      </i>
                     </div>

                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   domenica 31 ottobre 2010
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TM6zKM6E_NI/AAAAAAAAABk/OLQjzVNGoYM/s320/Lovecraft+10Lovecraft.JPG" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="8171684714129784186" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="5942782413973458811" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="5942782413973458811">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://2minutidodio.blogspot.it/2010/10/lovecraft-tec-ceramolle-20x15cm.html">
                      H.P. Lovecraft
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5942782413973458811" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TM6zKM6E_NI/AAAAAAAAABk/OLQjzVNGoYM/s1600/Lovecraft+10Lovecraft.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="320" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TM6zKM6E_NI/AAAAAAAAABk/OLQjzVNGoYM/s320/Lovecraft+10Lovecraft.JPG" width="243"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      "Lovecraft" 2010 Tec. Mista su tela 80x60 cm
                     </div>
                     <div class="" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TMy--gk146I/AAAAAAAAAAw/wOWMX1vSIU8/s1600/Lovecraft+.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="400" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TMy--gk146I/AAAAAAAAAAw/wOWMX1vSIU8/s400/Lovecraft+.JPG" width="281"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      "Lovecraft" 2010 Tec. ceramolle 20x15 cm (battitura)
                     </div>
                     <div class="" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TM60wqD-mII/AAAAAAAAABo/zot_EdauPL4/s1600/Caos+2caos.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="400" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_ENQMwkUthTA/TM60wqD-mII/AAAAAAAAABo/zot_EdauPL4/s400/Caos+2caos.JPG" width="276"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      "Caos" 2010 Tec. Collografia
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <span class="Apple-style-span" style="color: #2a2a2a; font-family: Tahoma, Verdana, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        Grattuggia le pietre morenti,
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        posizionate in modo spettrale...
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        L'ispirazione  la deviazione
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        mentale
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        dell'uomo saggio...
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        Fare un sacco di cose magnifiche,
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        assieme ad un sacco
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        di gente magnifica,
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        in un Mondo stramaledettamente
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        magnifico...
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        E quindi?
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        Dove sta l'imbroglio?
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        Non me lo spiego,
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        non riesco
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        a capire...
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        Piet per favore,
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        sono stanco,
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        lasciatemi in pace,
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        maledetti incubi...
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div style="line-height: 17px;">
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <i>
                        <span class="Apple-style-span" style="font-style: normal;">
                         "Disgusto"
                        </span>
                        <u>
                         Diego Zanoletti
                        </u>
                       </i>
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
